CREATE TABLE `promos` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `printed` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `location_id` int(11) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `redeemed` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `code` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `market_name` varchar(25) NOT NULL,
  `track_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `market_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `market_max_promo` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `market_initial_credits` int(2) NOT NULL,
  `credits` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `when` datetime NOT NULL,
  `updated` datetime NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `track_id` (`track_id`),
  KEY `market_id` (`market_id`),
  KEY `location_id` (`location_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2638 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
